# Blocker

# Description __

This object prevents passthrough while power is received through its second input.

Page views: 5,835  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __History](/rust/item/electric.cabletunnel~history)



# Cable Tunnel

# Description __

Allows you to pass a cable through a wall. Each input will forward the amount it receives to the corresponding output on the other side.

Page views: 6,242  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __History](/rust/item/electric.counter~history)



# Counter

# Description __

A basic cathode ray tube screen combined with an incremental counter. Can display power received, or can count upwards and allow passthrough when a target is reached.

Page views: 5,832  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Door Controller

# Description __

A Door Controller. Will manipulate the state of the closest door when it recieves power

Page views: 5,989  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Small Generator

# Description __

A small electric generator powered by Low Grade Fuel that outputs 40 power.

Page views: 6,067  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# HBHF Sensor

# Description __

A Heartbeat, Breathing, Humidity and Footstep sensor. Passthrough is equal to the number of humans detected in a 20m radius w/ LOS. Configurable w/ hammer

Page views: 10,284  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Igniter

# Description __

Ignites nearby objects such as furnaces and campfires when power is received

Page views: 9,964  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __History](/rust/item/electric.orswitch~history)



# OR Switch

# Description __

A logic gate that allows eletrical passthrough if EITHER input receives power, passthrough amount is the greater of either power source. Usage per unit: 1 ϟ(power).

Page views: 4,855  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Description __

A gate which allows power to flow while a player is standing on it

  * [ __History](/rust/item/electric.random.switch~history)



# RAND Switch

# Description __

This switch will allow passthrough based on a random number. Each time the SET input receives power it will roll true or false to allow passthrough

Page views: 4,723  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

#  [Rust Wiki](/rust/)

[Home](/rust/) / [Seismic Sensor](/rust/item/electric.seismicsensor)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/electric.seismicsensor)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/electric.seismicsensor~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/electric.seismicsensor~history)



# Seismic Sensor

# Description __

A small device that detects vibrations within a set range. Will output a different power value depending on the explosive type detected, ideal to know when your time has come.

  
  
  
  
  
  
  


# General Information __

  * **Identifier** 948291630
  * **Stack Size** ×10
  * **Despawn Time** 20 min
  * **HP** 200
  * **Power Usage** 1



Output 1

  * Homemade Landmine
  * F1 Grenade
  * Beancan Grenade
  * Incendiary Rocket
  * HV Rocket
  * Sam Ammo
  * Homing Missile
  * Patrol Helicopter (Rocket)
  * Bradley APC (Main Cannon)



Output 2

  * Satchel Charge
  * Explosive 5.56 Rifle Ammo
  * 40MM HE Grenade
  * Torpedo



Output 3

  * Timed Explosive Charge (C4)
  * Rocket
  * MLRS Rocket (untested)

# Large Solar Panel

# Description __

A solar panel which converts sunlight into energy. The amount of energy generated is dependent on the sun's intensity and angle to the panel.0-20(power)

Page views: 6,469  
Updated: This Year

  * [ __History](/rust/item/electric.splitter~history)



# Splitter

# Description __

Splits an electrical signal into 3 multiple signals. the amount passed through is equal to the input amount divided by the number of used output slots.

Page views: 5,009  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Description __

A Timer switch, will pass power through for duration.

[Home](/rust/) / [XOR Switch](/rust/item/electric.xorswitch)

  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/electric.xorswitch~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/electric.xorswitch~history)



# XOR Switch

# Description __

An exclusive-or logic gate that allows eletrical passthrough if ONLY ONE input receives power, passthrough amount is whichever single input is active. if BOTH inputs recieve power, passthrough will be zero. Usage per unit: 0 ϟ (power).

Page views: 4,677

# Electrical Branch

# Description __

This object allows you to branch power off from a main line by a set amount.

Page views: 5,519  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __View](/rust/item/electrical.combiner)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/electrical.combiner~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/electrical.combiner~history)



# Root Combiner

# Description __

This object combines two root electrical sources into a single signal. Helpful for stringing together low energy batteries or solar panels to produce higher power output. Can be wired in series, can not be used with any non energy producing electrical components.

Page views: 6,643  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

[Home](/rust/) / [Memory Cell](/rust/item/electrical.memorycell)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/electrical.memorycell)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/electrical.memorycell~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/electrical.memorycell~history)



# Memory Cell

# Description __

A 1 bit storage component. SET input will set the value to 1 CLEAR input sets the value to 0. Output will provide connected power if value is 1, Inverted output will provide connected power if value is 0. This is also known as a D-Type Flip Flop

Page views: 5,131  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Elevator

# Description __

A powered elevator. Place another elevator above or below this to connect it. Requires power.

  
  
  
  
  
  
  


# General Information __

  * **Identifier** 1177596584
  * **Stack Size** ×5
  * **Despawn Time** 40 min
  * **HP** 600
  * **Power Usage** 5
  * **Max Height** 11



Page views: 379  
Updated: This Year

  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/explosive.satchel~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/explosive.satchel~history)



# Satchel Charge

# Description __

Small explosive package constructed of beancan grenades. Useful for destroying wood and sheet metal doors.

Satchel charges have a chance to "dud" when thrown. Such satchels will not explose and instead require a player to interact with them. When this happens, the satchel is either placed back in the players inventory or reignites with a shorter fuse. You better get out of there!

Building Grade | Number of Satchels  
---|---  
twig | 1 (not recommended)  
Wood | 3  
Stone | 10  
Metal | 23  
Armored | 46  
Door Type | Number of Satchels  
---|---  
Wooden Door | 2  
Sheet Metal Door | 4  
Garage Door | 9  
Armored Door | 12  
  
Page views: 226,471  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

#  [Rust Wiki](/rust/)

[Home](/rust/) / [Timed Explosive Charge](/rust/item/explosive.timed)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/explosive.timed)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/explosive.timed~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/explosive.timed~history)



# Timed Explosive Charge

# Description __

C4, useful for breaking into bases.

C4 is expensive but reliable. Needs to be crafted at a [Workbench Level 3](/rust/item/workbench3)

Building Grade | Number of C4  
---|---  
twig | 1 (not recommended)  
Wood | 1  
Stone | 2  
Metal | 4  
Armored | 8  
Door Type | Number of C4  
---|---  
Wooden Door | 1(Not Recommended)  
Sheet Metal Door | 1  
Garage Door | 2  
Armored Door | 3  
  
# Crafting Costs __

Workbench Level 3 is required to craft this item.

Ingredients | Quantity  
---|---  
Explosives | x20  
Cloth | x5  
Tech Trash | x2  
  
Page views: 308,957  
Updated: This Month

# Explosives

# Description __

A component used for crafting C4 and Rockets.

Page views: 12,846
